Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCRM and Sales toolsFreshsales\nFreshsales\n\nWith Freshsales (formerly Freshworks CRM) modules in Make, you can watch, create, update, view, list, search, and delete contacts, leads, accounts, tasks, deals, notes, and sales activities in your Freshsales account.\n\nTo get started with Freshsales, create an account at freshworks.com/crm/sales.\n\nConnect Freshsales to Make\n\nTo connect your Freshsales account to Make you must obtain an API Key from your Freshsales account.\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\n1. Log in to your Freshsales account dashboard.\n\n2. Click on your Profile Icon > Settings > API Settings.\n\n3. In the API Settings tab, complete the authentication to view your API Key.\n\n4. Copy the API Key to your clipboard.\n\n5. Log in to your Make account, add a Freshsales module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\n6. Optional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n7. In the Choose an API URL Endpoint field, select your account URL format.\n\n8. In the Your CRM domain name field, enter the domain name. For example, if your Freshsales account accessing URL is www.xyz.myfreshworks.com/crm/sales, your domain is xyz.\n\n9. In the Your API Key field, paste the API Key copied in step 4 and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Freshsales modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up Freshsales Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. Webhook modules have an instant tag next to their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd a Freshsales instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your Freshsales account. and follow the Freshsales How to configure a workflow? guide. Use the following information in the Actions section:\n\nActions\n\n\t\n\nTrigger Webhooks\n\n\n\n\nRequest Method\n\n\t\n\nSelect your desired request method.\n\n\n\n\nCallback URL\n\n\t\n\nPaste the webhook URL you copied in step 4.\n\nFreshsales will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nLead\nWatch New Leads\nCreate a Lead\nUpdate a Lead\nView a You can create an account at insightly.com.\n\nRefer to the Insightly CRM API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Insightly CRM to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Insightly CRM.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Insightly CRM\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Insightly CRM account:\n\nLog in to your Insightly CRM account.\n\nClick the profile icon in the top right corner.\n\nClick User Settings.\n\nIn the API section, copy the Your API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Insightly CRM in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Insightly CRM module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Insightly CRM modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Insightly CRM Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nTriggers\n\nWatch objects\n\nActions\n\nCreate object\n\nRetrieve object\n\nInsightly CRM\nConnect Insightly CRM to Make\nObtain your API key in Insightly CRM\nEstablish the connection with Insightly CRM in Make\nBuild Insightly CRM Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationYodel.io\nYodel.io\nGetting Started with Yodel.io\n\nThe Yodel.io modules allow you to monitor inbound calls, outbound calls, finished calls, added tags, and removed tags in your Yodel.io account.\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Yodel.io account\n\nIn order to use Yodel.io with Make, it is necessary to have a Yodel.io account. If you do not have one, you can create a Yodel.io account at manage.yodel.io/sign_up.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Yodel.io to Make\n\nTo connect your Yodel.io account to Make the API Key must be obtained from your Yodel.io account.\n\n1. Open Integrations settings from the menu on the left.\n\n2. Add Make from the Available Integrations section by clicking the green button .\n\n3. Make now appears in the Installed Integrations section.\n\n4. Click on the View button to view and copy the generated token.\n\n5. Insert the copied token to the API Key field in the Create a connection dialog and save the dialog using the Continue button.\n\nThe connection between Yodel.io and Make is now established.\n\nNote\n\nFor information about making calls in Slack using Yodel.io please refer to the Yodel.io knowledge base.\n\nTriggers\nInbound Call\n\nTriggers when a call is incoming.\n\nWebhook\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the webhook for an inbound call.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the connection to your Yodel.io account.\n\nOutbound call\n\nTriggers when a call is outgoing.\n\nWebhook\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the webhook for an outbound call.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the connection to your Yodel.io account.\n\nCall Ended\n\nTriggers when a call is finished or was missed.\n\nWebhook\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the webhook for an ended call.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the connection to your Yodel.io account.\n\nTag Added\n\nTriggers when a tag is added to a call.\n\nWebhook\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the webhook for an added call.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the connection to your Yodel.io account.\n\nTag Removed\n\nTriggers when a tag is removed from a call.\n\nWebhook\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the webhook for a removed call.\n\nWebhook name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nSelect or add the connection to your Yodel.io account.\n\nYodel.io\nGetting Started with Yodel.io\nConnecting Yodel.io to Make\nTriggers\nInbound Call\nOutbound call\nCall Ended\nTag Added\nTag Removed\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationZoom\nZoom \n\nWith Zoom modules in Make, you can monitor, create, update, retrieve, or delete meetings and webinars, manage meeting and webinar registrants, or manage cloud recordings, phone calls, and chats in your Zoom account.\n\nTo get started with the Zoom app, create an account at zoom.us/signup.\n\nNote\n\nRefer to the Zoom API documentation for the list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Zoom to Make\nJWT App Type Deprecation\n\nZoom is deprecating the JWT app type and tokens. Existing connections using JWT tokens should be re-established using OAuth as soon as possible. Follow the procedures detailed in the sections below to establish a new OAuth connection and ensure your scenarios continue to run.\n\nPlease refer to the following timeline:\n\nJune 1, 2023: New JWT app types can no longer be created.\n\nSeptember 1, 2023: JWT apps and their tokens will be disabled by Zoom.\n\nFor additional information, refer to the Zoom API Documentation.\n\nTo connect to the Zoom app:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Zoom module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook > Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. To create these values, see the Create Custom App and Client Credentials in Zoom section.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access in the popup window.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Zoom modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate Custom App and Client Credentials in Zoom\n\nYou can create your own application and connect it to Make using the App ID and Secret values from the application.\n\nGo to marketplace.zoom.us and log in to your account.\n\nClick Develop > Build App > OAuth > Create.\n\nEnter your App Name, select Account-level app, choose if you would like the app published on the Zoom App Marketplace, and click Create.\n\nEnter the following details on the App credentials page and click Continue.\n\nRedirect URL for OAuth\n\n\t\n\nhttps://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/zoom2\n\n\n\n\nAdd Allow Lists\n\n\t\n\nhttps://www.make.com\n\nhttps://www.integromat.com\n\nNote\n\nPlease ensure to whitelist the following URL address as it may effect the connection: https://www.integromat.com.\n\nEnter the Basic information for the app.\n\nApp name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the app.\n\n\n\n\nShort Description\n\n\t\n\nEnter a short description of the app.\n\n\n\n\nLong Description\n\n\t\n\nEnter a long description of the app.\n\n\n\n\nPreview Content\n\n\t\n\nAdd images to show the app's content. You can upload a maximum of six images. If you are uploading a video, then you can upload a maximum of five images and a video.\n\n\n\n\nCompany Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the company app. This name will appear on the marketplace homepage and on the app’s detail page.\n\n\n\n\nCategory\n\n\t\n\nSelect up to three categories for your app.\n\n\n\n\nIndustrial Vertical\n\n\t\n\nSelect a vertical if your app has been built with industry vertical-specific compliance such as HIPAA, FedRAMP, or is specific to Higher Education or K-12.\n\n\n\n\nMarket Segment\n\n\t\n\nAdd one or more relevant market segments for your app.\n\n\n\n\nLine of Business\n\n\t\n\nAdd one or more relevant lines of business for your app.\n\n\n\n\nDeveloper Contact Information\n\n\t\n\nAdd the developer's details:\n\nName: Enter the name of the developer.\n\nEmail address: Enter the email address of the developer.\n\n\n\n\nLinks\n\n\t\n\nAdd the following links:\n\nPrivate Policy URL: Provide a URL link to your Privacy Policy that must comply with applicable laws and regulations and that make clear how you collect, use, share, retain and otherwise process personal information.\n\nTerms of use URL: Provide the URL for your app’s Terms of Use agreement.\n\nSupport URL: Provide a URL link to your app's support page that users can use to get direct support from your team in regards to this integration.\n\nSelect desired subscriptions for the app on the Feature page and click Continue.\n\nClick Add Scopes on the Scopes page, select the desired scopes for your app, and click Continue. For example, meetings, users, etc.\n\nNote\n\nYou must add scopes for users to establish the connection and keep the app private.\n\nOn the left menu, click App credentials, copy the Client ID and Client secret, and store them in a safe place.\n\nYou now have the client credentials to connect to Make.\n\nMeeting\nWatch Meetings\nCreate a Meeting\nGet a Meeting\nList Meetings\nUpdate a Meeting\nEnd a Meeting\nDelete a Meeting\nAdd a Meeting Registrant\nList Meeting Registrants\nUpdate Meeting Registrants Status\nWebinar\nWatch Webinars\nCreate a Webinar\nGet a Webinar\nList Webinars\nUpdate a Webinar\nDelete a Webinar\nAdd a Webinar Registrant\nList Webinar Registrants\nUpdate Webinar Registrant Status\nAdd Webinar Panelist\nList Webinar Panelist\nRemove a Webinar Panelist\nCloud Recording\nCaution\n\nRequires a Pro or higher plan and cloud recording must be enabled on the user’s account.\n\nWatch Recordings\nList Cloud Recordings\nDownload a Cloud Recording\nDelete a Cloud Recording\nPhone Call\nWatch Phone Calls\nList Phone Numbers\nList Call Logs\nChat\nWatch Chat Channels\nWatch Chat Messages\nSend a Chat Message\nUser\nWatch User Activities\nOther\nMake an API Call\nUninstalling the Make App From a Zoom Account\n\n1. upsert, retrieve, search, and delete organizations\n\ncreate, update, upsert, retrieve, search, and delete people\n\ncreate, list, and delete products\n\ncreate, update, retrieve, search, and lists deals for organization and persons\n\ncreate and search tasks for a person, organization, and deal.\n\nTo get started with Agendor, create an account at agendor.com.\n\nConnect Agendor to Make\n\nTo connect Agendor app, you need to obtain the API Key.\n\nLog in to your Agendor account.\n\nClick apps Menu > Integrations, and copy the API Key to a safe place.\n\nLog in to your Make account, insert an Agendor module scenario and click the Add button next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the details copied in step 2 and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully connected the Agendor app and can now build scenarios.\n\nOrganizations\n\nYou can create, update, upsert, retrieve, search, and delete organizations management\nInternet of Things\nIT and Development\nLanguage Tools\nLifestyle\nMarketing\nProductivity\nProcess Management\nSurveys and Forms\nTravel\nWebsite Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationWhatsApp Business Cloud\nWhatsApp Business Cloud \n\nWith WhatsApp Business Cloud modules in Make, you can:\n\nwatch events, send a message, and template messages\n\nupload and download media\n\nenable two-step verification, register, verify, and deregister senders\n\nretrieve and update business profiles\n\nCaution\n\nPlease note that it is not possible to use the phone number registered in the WhatsApp Business app or your personal WhatsApp number, which you use for communicating with friends and family. You will need a separate dedicated phone number for the API. For more information, please refer to the Could API documentation.\n\nTo get started with WhatsApp Business Cloud, you need:\n\nA Facebook Developer account\n\nA valid mobile phone number.\n\nNote\n\nBefore you begin, understand the following information about the phone numbers:\n\nThe phone number should not be registered with your personal WhatsApp account which you use to communicate with your friends and family. If already registered, delete the existing account on your mobile to register with WhatsApp Business Cloud.\n\nYou cannot use the same phone number simultaneously on both on-premise and Cloud API at the same time. Only one platform is supported at a time with the phone number. See overview and phone numbers.\n\nDo not infringe the WhatsApp Terms and Conditions: \"If you use anything other than the official WhatsApp Business Platform or other official WhatsApp tools, We reserve the right to limit or remove your access to WhatsApp as this violates our policies. Please do not use any non-WhatsApp authorized third-party tools to communicate on WhatsApp. See Unauthorized use of automated or bulk messaging on WhatsApp for more information\".\n\nTo connect WhatsApp Cloud API to Make involves the following steps:\n\nSet Up WhatsApp Cloud API\n\nCreate Permanent Access Token\n\nConnect WhatsApp Business Cloud to Make\n\nSet Up WhatsApp Cloud API\n\nTo set up WhatsApp Cloud API:\n\nLog in to your Facebook account.\n\nGo to the Facebook Developer Site, click My Apps > Create App.\n\nSelect Business as the app type. Click Next.\n\nEnter the display name and select the business account. Click Create app.\n\nWhen prompted, re-enter the password of your Facebook account. Click Submit.\n\nThe app is created.\n\nOn the app's Dashboard, scroll down to find the WhatsApp app, and click Set up.\n\nSelect the account type, and click Continue.\n\nCopy the WhatsApp Business Account ID to a safe place.\n\nCreate Permanent Access Token\n\nTo create a permanent access token for your WhatsApp Business Cloud account:\n\nLog in to your Facebook Developer Account.\n\nClick Apps Dashboard > Business Settings.\n\nNote\n\nIf you don't see the App Dashboard menu, refresh the page.\n\nGo to System Users > Add. Enter the username, select the role as Admin and click Create System User.\n\nGo to Add Assets > Apps. Select the app you want to assign to the user, enable Full Control access, and click Save Changes.\n\nGo to WhatsApp Accounts > Add People > Select the system user > Enable Full Control Access > Assign.\n\nGo to System Users > Select the user > Generate Access Token.\n\nSelect the app, following permissions, and then click Generate Token.\n\nwhatsapp_business_messaging\n\nwhatsapp_business_management\n\nCopy the token to a safe place.\n\nYou can use this token as a permanent access token.\n\nAdd your own phone number to WhatsApp Business Cloud API\n\nWhen you set up WhatsApp API, a test number is created for you. You can add your own number.\n\nLog in to your Facebook developer account.\n\nOn the Getting Started page, click Add phone number.\n\nEnter your business profile details and click Next.\n\nEnter the business phone number that you want to connect to WhatsApp Business API.\n\nNote\n\nEnsure that the phone number is not registered with WhatsApp before. If already registered, delete your WhatsApp account with the number before registering here.\n\nEnter the verification code received on your phone number.\n\nEnter your business details and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully added your own business phone number to WhatsApp Business Cloud API.\n\nConnect WhatsApp Business Cloud to Make\n\nTo connect WhatsApp Business Cloud with Make you need to obtain the Permanent Token and WhatsApp Business Account ID values from your WhatsApp Business Cloud account.\n\nIn your Facebook developer account:\n\nSet up WhatsApp Business Cloud API\n\nCreate a permanent access token\n\nLog in to your Make account, and add a module from the WhatsApp Business Cloud app into a Make scenario.\n\nClick Add next to the Connection field.\n\nIn the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the Permanent Token field, enter the token created prior to the connection.\n\nYou can also use a temporary token which is only valid for 24 hours and available on the getting started screen.\n\nNote\n\nMake recommends using the temporary token for testing purposes as it is valid only for 24 hours and you will lose your data once the token expires.\n\nIn the WhatsApp Business Account ID field, enter the ID from your Facebook Developer account > WhatsApp > Getting Started section screen, and click Save.\n\nYou have successfully connected the WhatsApp Business Cloud app and can now build scenarios.\n\nMessage\n\nYou can watch events, and send messages using the following modules.\n\nWatch Events\nSend a Message\nSend a Template Message\nMedia\n\nYou can upload and download media using the following modules.\n\nUpload a Media\nDownload a Media\nPhone Number\n\nYou can enable two-step verification, register, verify, and deregister senders using the following modules.\n\nEnable Two-Step Verification\nRegister a Sender\nVerify a Sender\nDeregister a Sender\nBusiness Profile\n\nYou can retrieve and update business profiles using the following modules.\n\nGet a Business Profile\nUpdate a Business Profile\nSetting up WhatsApp Business Cloud webhooks\nAdd Recipient's Phone Number\nTroubleshooting the WhatsApp Business Cloud\n\nSome of the errors that you might encounter when using WhatsApp Business Cloud.\n\nWhatsApp API - Error 500 code 13100\n\nThe user gets an error 500 from the module and the DevTool > Response Body shows error code 131000.\n\nNote\n\nYou can only initiate new chats via Send a Template module. Only after sending a templated message to a specific customer and receiving a response from the customer, you can use this Send a Message module to send a non-templated message to the customer.\n\nIf you’re using a testing number, you must first register up to five authorized recipient numbers in WhatsApp Manager before sending messages to them. See Add Recipient's Phone Number.\n\nWhatsApp Business Cloud\nSet Up WhatsApp Cloud API\nCreate Permanent Access Token\nAdd your own phone number to WhatsApp Business Cloud API\nConnect WhatsApp Business Cloud to Make\nMessage\nWatch Events\nSend a Message\nSend a Template Message\nMedia\nUpload a Media\nDownload a Media\nPhone Number\nEnable Two-Step Verification\nRegister a Sender\nVerify a Sender\nDeregister a Sender\nBusiness Profile\nGet a Business Profile\nUpdate a Business Profile\nSetting up WhatsApp Business Cloud webhooks\nAdd Recipient's Phone Number\nTroubleshooting the WhatsApp Business Cloud\nWhatsApp API - Error 500 code 13100\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationZoho Mail\nZoho Mail\nGetting Started with Zoho Mail\n\nThe Zoho Mail modules allow you to monitor emails, create emails, tasks, send emails, and retrieve email details in your Zoho CRM account.\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Zoho account\n\nIn order to use Zoho Mail with Make, it is necessary to have a Zoho Mail account. If you do not have one, you can create a Zoho Mail account at www.zoho.com/mail/.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Zoho Mail to Make\n\nTo connect your Zoho Mail account to Make follow the general instructions for Connecting to Services.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Zoho Mail website where you will be prompted to grant Makeaccess to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Accept button.\n\nThe connection to your Zoho Mail account has been established.\n\nConnecting Zoho Mail to Make (Advanced)\n\nTo connect your Zoho Mail account to Make you need to retrieve the Client ID and Client Secret.\n\nGo to https://accounts.zoho.eu/developerconsole and sign in.\n\nClick on the Add Client ID button.\n\nEnter the required data. Enter https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/zoho-mail to the Authorized redirect URIs field.\n\nSave the provided Client ID and Client Secret.\n\nOpen Make and the Zoho Mail module's Create a connection dialog.\n\nSelect the correct region of your Zoho Mail account.\n\nClick on Show advanced settings.\n\nEnter the Client ID and the Client Secret you have retrieved in the steps above.\n\nClick on the Continue button.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Zoho website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Accept button.\n\nThe connection to your Zoho Mail account is now established.\n\nZoho Mail\nGetting Started with Zoho Mail\nConnecting Zoho Mail to Make\nConnecting Zoho Mail to Make (Advanced)\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationWebex Meetings\nWebex Meetings\n\nThe Webex Meetings modules enable you to monitor started meetings or perform an API call in your Webex Meetings account.\n\nGetting Started with Webex Meetings\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Webex Meetings account — you can create one at www.webex.com/video-conferencing.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Webex Meetings to Make\n\n1. Go to Make and open the Webex Meetings module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n2. Enter a name for the connection to the Connection name field and click Continue.\n\nAfter you click the Continue button, Make will redirect you to the Webex Meetings website where you will be prompted to grant Make access to your account.\n\nConfirm the dialog by clicking the Accepts button.\n\nMeetings\nWatch Meeting Started\n\nRetrieves meeting details when a meeting has started.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Webex Meetings account.\n\n\n\n\nFrom\n\n\t\n\nEnter the start date and time (inclusive) for the range for which meetings are to be returned. See the supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nTo\n\n\t\n\nEnter the end date and time (exclusive) for the range for which meetings are to be returned. See the supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of meetings Make will return during one execution cycle.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nAllows you to perform a custom API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Webex Meetings account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://webexapis.com.For example: /v1/meetings.\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Webex Meetings API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST to create a new entry.\n\nPUT to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we added those for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Meetings\n\nThe following API call returns all meetings in your Webex Meetings account:\n\nURL: /v1/meetings\n\nMethod: GET\n\nThe result can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > items. In our example, 2 meetings were returned:\n\nWebex Meetings\nGetting Started with Webex Meetings\nConnecting Webex Meetings to Make\nMeetings\nWatch Meeting Started\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Meetings\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationWeChat Official Account\nWeChat Official Account\n\nWith WeChat modules in Make, you can manage all your messaging, assets, tags, and users, generate QR codes, and make API calls in your WeChat Official Account.\n\nTo get started, create a WeChat Official Account. You must register your WeChat Official Account under an Overseas Business Entity and select from two different types of accounts. Please follow this application procedure and learn more about the process, requirements, fees, and rules.\n\nConnecting WeChat to Make\n\nTo make a connection you need an App ID and App Secret from your WeChat Official Account.\n\nLog in to your WeChat Official Account.\n\nGo to the WeChat public platform.\n\nScan the QR code with the scanner in your WeChat app (other barcode scanning apps will not work).\n\nClick Accept on your phone and the website redirects you.\n\nYou should now see your App ID and App Secret under Test number information. Copy these to your clipboard.\n\nGo to your Make scenario and select the WeChat Official Account module you want to use.\n\nUnder Connection, click Add.\n\nGive your new connection a name.\n\nPaste the App ID and App Secret in the fields below.\n\nClick Save.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection.\n\nWebhook configuration\n\nThe Watch Messages module allows you to monitor for incoming messages and trigger a scenario.\n\nGo to your Make scenario and select the Watch Messages module.\n\nYou can put any random string in Token but remember to write it down. This token is for webhook validation.\n\nClick Save and copy the webhook address to your clipboard.\n\nSave the scenario and refresh the page.\n\nGo back to your WeChat Official Account and click modification under the title Interface configuration information.\n\nPaste the webhook URL and the token, then click submit. If an error message appears, make sure you have pasted the correct webhook address and token.\n\nTo perform a test, add a Send a Message module and configure as follows.\n\nThen you should get a message after you send a message to your WeChat Official Account.\n\nYou have successfully configured the webhook.\n\nWeChat Official Account\nConnecting WeChat to Make\nWebhook configuration\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationToky\nToky\n\nThe Toky modules allow you to create, update, list, and retrieve the agents, contacts, text messages, and voicemails in your Toky account.\n\nGetting Started with Toky\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Toky account\n\nIn order to use Toky with Make, it is necessary to have a Toky account. If you do not have one, you can create a Toky account at app.toky.co/signup?.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Toky as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nConnecting Toky to Make\n\nTo connect your Toky account to Make you need to obtain the API Key from your Toky account and insert it in the Create a connection dialog in the Make module.\n\n1. Log in to your Toky account and open your Dashboard.\n\n2. Click Your Profile Icon > API Keys > Show > Copy and Close.\n\n3. Go to Make and open the Create a connection dialog.\n\n4. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n5. In the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 2, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nAgents\nList Agents\n\nRetrieves all agents from a Toky account.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of agent Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nContacts\nList Contacts\n\nGets all contacts from the phone directory.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of contacts Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nGet a Contact\n\nGets contact.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nPhone Number\n\n\t\n\nSelect the phone number whose contact details you want to retrieve.\n\nCreate a Contact\n\nCreates a new contact in the phone directory.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nCreated By\n\n\t\n\nSelect the member's email address who is creating the contact.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nLast Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the last name of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nPhone Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the phone number of the contact including the country code. For example, +17564043678.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address of the contact.\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nUpdates contact.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nPhone Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the phone number of the contact whose details you want to update.\n\n\n\n\nFirst Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the first name of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nLast Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the last name of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address of the contact.\n\n\n\n\nCompany Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the company name to which the contact is associated with.\n\nText Messages\nWatch New Text Messages\n\nTriggers when there is a new incoming text message in Toky.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Toky as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\nList Text Messages\n\nList text messages history sent, and received. The result is ordered by descending date.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of text messages Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nCreate a Text Message.\n\nSends a text message.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nFrom\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Toky number from which you want to send the SMS. It must be an SMS enabled number.\n\n\n\n\nTo\n\n\t\n\nEnter the number to which you want to send the SMS.\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter the message text you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nEmail\n\n\t\n\nEnter the email address of the Toky agent who is sending the message.\n\nCalls\nWatch New Calls\n\nTriggers when there is a new call in the Toky.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Toky as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\nVoicemails\nWatch New Calls\n\nTriggers when there is a new voicemail in the Toky.\n\nNote\n\nYou do not have to add the webhooks in the Toky as it is automatically done for you once you add and save an instant trigger module to your scenario.\n\nWebhook Name\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name of the webhook.\n\n\n\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\nList Voicemails\n\nList voicemail history. The result is ordered by descending created date.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nLimit\n\n\t\n\nSet the maximum number of voicemails Make should return during one scenario execution cycle.\n\nGet a Voicemails\n\nRetrieves voicemail recording URL with ID of the voicemail.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nVoicemail ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Voicemail ID whose details you want to retrieve.\n\nOther\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Toky account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://api.toky.co/. For example: /v1/contacts\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Toky API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST to create a new entry.\n\nPUT to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - Get contacts\n\nThe following API call returns all contacts from your Toky account:\n\nURL: /v1/contacts\n\nMethod: GET\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body > results. In our example, 3 contacts were returned:\n\nToky\nGetting Started with Toky\nConnecting Toky to Make\nAgents\nList Agents\nContacts\nList Contacts\nGet a Contact\nCreate a Contact\nUpdate a Contact\nText Messages\nWatch New Text Messages\nList Text Messages\nCreate a Text Message.\nCalls\nWatch New Calls\nVoicemails\nWatch New Calls\nList Voicemails\nGet a Voicemails\nOther\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - Get contacts\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationTwilio\nTwilio\n\nWith Twilio modules in Make, you can manage the messages, calls, recording, transcriptions, notifications, and executions in your Twilio account.\n\nTo use the Twilio modules, you must have a Twilio account. You can create an account at login.twilio.com/u/signup.\n\nNote\n\nIf you have a free account, you can only send messages and make calls to verified phone numbers.\n\nRefer to the Twilio API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Twilio to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your SID and Auth Token in Twilio.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your SID and Auth Token in Twilio\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Twilio account:\n\nLog in to your Twilio account.\n\nGo to Dashboard > the Developer tab.\n\nIn the Account info section, copy your Account SID and Auth Token and store them in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the SID and Auth Token field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Twilio in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Twilio module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nNote: If you add a module with an instant tag, click Create a webhook, then Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the SID field, enter the Account SID copied in the section above.\n\nIn the Auth Token field, enter the Auth Token copied in the section above.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Twilio modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Twilio Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nMessages\n\nWatch Messages\n\nCreate a Message\n\nNote: You need a Twilio phone number. To find it, sign in to your Twilio account, go to Dashboard > Develop tab. In the Account info section, copy your Twilio phone number.\n\nIn the Status callback field, insert the webhook that you should create in the New Message Status Event module.\n\nList Messages\n\nGet a Message\n\nDelete a Message\n\nList Message Media\n\nDownload a Media Resource\n\nCalls\n\nWatch Calls\n\nCreate a Call\n\nList Calls\n\nGet a Call\n\nDelete a Call\n\nRecordings\n\nWatch Recordings\n\nDownload a Recording Media\n\nList Recording Transcription\n\nTranscriptions\n\nWatch Transcriptions\n\nNotifications\n\nWatch Alerts\n\nNote: Twilio doesn't support queries for alerts older than 30 days.\n\nCallback Webhooks\n\nNew Message Status Event\n\nNote: Triggers when a message status is changed to queued, failed, sent, delivered, or undelivered.\n\nTip\n\nCopy the webhook link and paste it to the Status callback field in the Create a Message module.\n\nExecution\n\nCreate an Execution\n\nGet an Execution\n\nUpdate an Execution\n\nDelete an Execution\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nMake an API Call for Studio\n\nTwilio\nConnect Twilio to Make\nObtain your SID and Auth Token in Twilio\nBuild Twilio Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationTelegram Bot\nTelegram Bot\n\nWith the Telegram Bot modules in Make, you can:\n\nedit, forward, delete, pin, and unpin messages, and send text message or replies\n\nsend audio files, documents, images, albums, photos, stickers, videos, video notes, voice messages, and invoices\n\nsend media by URL or ID\n\nedit media messages, and message captions\n\ndownload files\n\ncreate, revoke, and edit chat invite links\n\nwatch, and list updates, and chats\n\nkick, promote, and restrict chat members\n\nlist administrators in a chat\n\nretrieve number of members in chat\n\ncall APIs\n\nanswer inline queries\n\nGetting Started with Telegram Bot\nPrerequisites\n\nA configured Bot via Telegram app. You can download the Telegram Desktop app at desktop.telegram.org.\n\nIn order to use the Telegram app, your mobile phone number has to be provided.\n\nConfiguring the Telegram Bot\n\n1. Go to https://telegram.me/BotFather.\n\n2. To create a new bot type /newbot to the message box and press enter.\n\n3. Enter the name of the user name of your new bot.\n\nYou have received the message from BotFather containing the token, which you can use to connect Telegram Bot to Make.\n\nTo add your bot to your Telegram application, click the link in the message from BotFather or enter it manually to your browser. The link is t.me/yourBotName.\n\nAdding Telegram Bot to your Scenario\n\nFollow Step 1 in the Creating a scenario article (choose the Telegram Bot module instead of Twitter and Facebook module).\n\nAfter the module is added to your scenario you can then see the Scenario editor.\n\nDefine what function you need your module to have. Here you can choose between three types of modules – Triggers, Actions, and Searches.\n\nDid you know?\n\nYou can find a lot of sample scenario templates with Telegram Bot modules at www.make.com/en/integrations/telegram.\n\nMessages\n\nSend a Text Message or Reply\n\nSends a text message or a reply to your Telegram Desktop application.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nUser ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the UserID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter (or map) the text content of the message you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nMessage Thread ID\n\n\t\n\nA Unique identifier for the forum's target message thread (topic). Applicable for forum supergroups only.\n\n\n\n\nParse mode\n\n\t\n\nSpecify how you want your text to be recognized. HTML or Markdown.\n\nMarkdown syntax:\n\n*bold text*\n_italic text_\n[inline URL](http://www.example.com/)\n[inline mention of a user](tg://user?id=123456789)\n`inline fixed-width code`\n```block_language\npre-formatted fixed-width code block\n```\n\n\nHTML syntax:\n\n<b>bold</b>, <strong>bold</strong>\n<i>italic</i>, <em>italic</em>\n<a href=\"http://www.example.com/\">inline URL</a>\n<a href=\"tg://user?id=123456789\">inline mention of a user</a>\n<code>inline fixed-width code</code>\n<pre>pre-formatted fixed-width code block</pre>\n\n\n\n\nDisable Notifications\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to send messages silently. iOS users will not receive a notification; Android users will receive a notification with no sound.\n\n\n\n\nDisable Link Previews\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to disable link previews for links in this message.\n\n\n\n\nOriginal Message ID\n\n\t\n\nThe ID of the original message if the message is a reply.\n\n\n\n\nEnter/Assemble the Reply Markup Field\n\n\t\n\nEnter additional interface options that are a JSON-serialized object for an inline keyboard, custom reply keyboard, instructions to remove reply keyboard or to force a reply from the user, e.g.:\n\n{\"inline_keyboard\":[[{\"text\":\"Some button text 2\",\"url\":\"https://botpress.org\"}]]} or {\"keyboard\":[[\"Yes\",\"No\"],[\"Maybe\"]]}\n\nMore information about custom keyboards can be found on the Telegram Bot API page.\n\n\n\n\nReply Markup\n\n\t\n\nEnter additional interface options that are a JSON-serialized object, including an inline keyboard, a custom reply keyboard, instructions to remove the reply keyboard, or instructions to force a reply from the user, e.g. {\"inline_keyboard\":[[{\"text\":\"Some button text 2\",\"url\":\"https://botpress.org\"}]]} or {\"keyboard\":[[\"Yes\",\"No\"],[\"Maybe\"]]}.\n\nNote\n\nThe keyboard cannot be used with channels.\n\nEdit a Text Message\n\nEdits text or game messages.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nEdit\n\n\t\n\nSelect the message type you want to edit.\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nMessage ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Message ID you want to forward.\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter (or map) the text content of the message you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nParse mode\n\n\t\n\nSpecify how you want your text to be recognized. HTML or Markdown.\n\nMarkdown syntax:\n\n*bold text*\n_italic text_\n[inline URL](http://www.example.com/)\n[inline mention of a user](tg://user?id=123456789)\n`inline fixed-width code`\n```block_language\npre-formatted fixed-width code block\n```\n\nHTML syntax:\n\n<b>bold</b>, <strong>bold</strong>\n<i>italic</i>, <em>italic</em>\n<a href=\"http://www.example.com/\">inline URL</a>\n<a href=\"tg://user?id=123456789\">inline mention of a user</a>\n<code>inline fixed-width code</code>\n<pre>pre-formatted fixed-width code block</pre>\n\n\n\nDisable Link Previews\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to disable link previews.\n\n\n\n\nEnter/Assemble the Reply Markup Field\n\n\t\n\nEnter additional interface options that are a JSON-serialized object for an inline keyboard, custom reply keyboard, instructions to remove reply keyboard or to force a reply from the user, e.g.:\n\n{\"inline_keyboard\":[[{\"text\":\"Some button text 2\",\"url\":\"https://botpress.org\"}]]} or {\"keyboard\":[[\"Yes\",\"No\"],[\"Maybe\"]]}\n\nMore information about custom keyboards can be found on the Telegram Bot API page.\n\n\n\n\nReply Markup\n\n\t\n\nEnter additional interface options that are a JSON-serialized object for an inline keyboard, custom reply keyboard, instructions to remove reply keyboard or to force a reply from the user, e.g.:\n\n {\"inline_keyboard\":[[{\"text\":\"Some button text 2\",\"url\":\"https://botpress.org\"}]]} or {\"keyboard\":[[\"Yes\",\"No\"],[\"Maybe\"]]} \n\nMore information about custom keyboards can be found on the Telegram Bot API page.\n\nNote\n\nKeyboards cannot be used with channels.\n\nForward a Message\n\nForwards messages of any kind. This module can be used to forward messages only within Telegram.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nFrom chat ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Chat ID where the original message was sent (or channel username in the format @channelusername).\n\n\n\n\nMessage ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the message ID of the message you want to forward in the from_chat_id format.\n\n\n\n\nDisable Notifications\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to send the message silently. iOS users will not receive a notification; Android users will receive a notification with no sound.\n\nDelete a Message\n\nDeletes a message. A message can only be deleted if it was sent less than 48 hours ago.\n\nCaution\n\nOnly a message sent less than 48 hours ago can be deleted.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nMessage ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Message ID.\n\nPin a Message\nUnpin a Message\nMedia\n\nSend an Audio File\nSend a Document or an Image\nSend an Album\nSend a Photo\nSend a Sticker\nSend a Video\n\nSends a video file to your Telegram Desktop Application.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nMessage Thread ID\n\n\t\n\nA unique identifier for the target message thread (topic) of the forum. For forum supergroups only.\n\n\n\n\nCaption\n\n\t\n\nEnter the caption of the video.\n\n\n\n\nSend by\n\n\t\n\nImage file to send. Further details about sending files can be found on the Telegram Bot API page.\n\n\n\n\nDisable notification\n\n\t\n\nSelect Yes to send messages silently. iOS users will not receive a notification, Android users will receive a notification with no sound.\n\n\n\n\nContent type\n\n\t\n\nSelect or enter the MIME type of data.\n\n\n\n\nDuration\n\n\t\n\nEnter the duration of the video sent in seconds.\n\n\n\n\nWidth\n\n\t\n\nEnter the video width.\n\n\n\n\nHeight\n\n\t\n\nEnter the video height.\n\n\n\n\nEnter/Assemble the Reply Markup Field\n\n\t\n\nSelect if to enter or assemble the reply markup field.\n\n\n\n\nReply Markup\n\n\t\n\nEnter additional interface options that are a JSON-serialized object for an inline keyboard, custom reply keyboard, instructions to remove reply keyboard or to force a reply from the user, e.g.:\n\n {\"inline_keyboard\":[[{\"text\":\"Some button text 2\",\"url\":\"https://botpress.org\"}]]} or {\"keyboard\":[[\"Yes\",\"No\"],[\"Maybe\"]]}\n\nMore information about custom keyboards can be found on the Telegram Bot API page.\n\nSend a Video Note\nSend a Voice Message\nEdit a Media Message\nEdit a Message Caption\nSend an Invoice\nSend media by URL or ID\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Telegram Bot using the provided token\n\n\n\n\nChat ID\n\n\t\n\nTo set the Chat ID, follow these instructions\n\n\n\n\nMedia type\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to edit a photo or video.\n\n\n\n\nCaption\n\n\t\n\nEnter the photo/video caption.\n\n\n\n\nSend by\n\n\t\n\nSelect a file. Use the token provided by the BotFather (see the steps above, Configuring the Telegram Bot).\n\nThe connection between Telegram Bot and Make is now established. You can continue with other Telegram Bot actions.\n\nMembers\n\nUsing the following modules, you can list administrators, retrieve members, kick, promote, and restrict chat members.\n\nList Administrators in a Chat\nGet the Number of Members in a Chat\nKick a Chat Member\nPromote a Chat Member\nRestrict a Chat Member\nOther\n\nUsing the following modules, you can call APIs, and answer inline queries.\n\nMake an API Call\nAnswer an inline Query\nTroubleshooting\n\nCheck the following procedures if you are facing difficulties when using the Telegram bot app.\n\nHow to find out the ID of a private channel/group:\n\nOne possible way to determine the ID of a private channel/group is as follows:\n\nCreate a new scenario\n\nPlace Telegram Bot >; Watch updates module in the scenario.\n\nConfigure the module by creating a webhook.\n\nExecute the scenario.\n\nSend a message to the private channel/group.\n\nVerify the output of the module by clicking the bubble above the module.\n\nFind the ID in the output bundle:\n\nHow to find out the user ID\n\nTo find out the ID of a Telegram user, forward their message to the userinfobot. Check out the following procedure for steps on how to do that:\n\nAdd the userinfobot to your Telegram app. You can do that by entering @userinfobot in the search bar and selecting the userinfobot.\n\nGo to the chat with the user you want to retrieve the ID from.\n\nForward his message to userinfobot.\n\nCopy the User ID and paste it to the Make module.\n\nAdding Your Bot To the Channel:\n\nClick the right mouse button on the channel name and select the View channel info option.\n\nClick the Add Member icon next to the member number.\n\nStart typing the name of your bot in the search field.\n\nClick on the bot name to select the bot you want to add to the channel.\n\nClick the INVITE button.\n\nMake the bot admin by clicking the respective button.\n\nAssign the permissions to your bot and click the SAVE button.\n\nThe bot has been added to the channel.\n\nTesting a Public Channel\n\nTo test the public channel you need to obtain the Chat ID. The Chat ID is part of the channel link.\n\nThe channel name is NOT the channel link/chat ID.\n\nIf the public channel link is, for example, t.me/IMTtest, then @IMTtest is your Chat ID.\n\nNow, you can send a message to the public channel using the Send a Text Message or a Reply module.\n\nTesting a Private Channel:\n\nYou need to obtain the Chat ID to test the private channel. There are three options to retrieve the ID:\n\nRetrieve the ID from the web version of Telegram.\n\nSwitch the private channel to the public channel, then retrieve the ID (by sending or receiving the message in Make) and switch back the channel type to private.\n\nInvite the bot get_id_bot to your private channel and using the /my_id@get_id_bot command.\n\nRetrieving the ID From the Web Version of Telegram\n\nLog in to your Telegram account via https://web.telegram.org.\n\nClick on the private channel you want to retrieve the chat ID for.\n\nCopy the number between the c letter and the underscore from the URL. If the URL is https://web.telegram.org/#/im?p=c1424271061_11793697872942794544 then copy the 1424271061\n\nPaste the number to the desired field and add the prefix-100\n\nThe Chat ID of the private channel is then -1001424271061.\n\nYou can now use the ID in the desired Telegram Bot module in Make.\n\nRegistration and Login\n\nIt is not required. You can sign in on the site, telegram.org/auth where you can change your public settings. You will receive a key in your desktop application to submit your login.\n\nMy bot is hitting limits, how do I avoid this?\n\nWhen sending messages inside a particular chat, avoid sending more than one message per second. We may allow short bursts that go over this limit, but eventually you'll begin receiving 429 errors.\n\nIf you're sending bulk notifications to multiple users, the API will not allow more than 30 messages per second or so. Consider spreading out notifications over large intervals of 8—12 hours for best results.\n\nAlso note that your bot will not be able to send more than 20 messages per minute to the same group.\n\n(source: https://core.telegram.org/bots/faq#my-bot-is-hitting-limits-how-do-i-avoid-this)\n\nTelegram Bot\nGetting Started with Telegram Bot\nPrerequisites\nConfiguring the Telegram Bot\nAdding Telegram Bot to your Scenario\nDid you know?\nMessages\nSend a Text Message or Reply\nEdit a Text Message\nForward a Message\nDelete a Message\nPin a Message\nUnpin a Message\nMedia\nSend an Audio File\nSend a Document or an Image\nSend an Album\nSend a Photo\nSend a Sticker\nSend a Video\nSend a Video Note\nSend a Voice Message\nEdit a Media Message\nEdit a Message Caption\nSend an Invoice\nSend media by URL or ID\nDownload a File\nChats and Updates\nCreate a Chat Invite Link\nEdit a Chat Invite Link\nList Updates\nList Chats\nRevoke a Chat Invite Link\nWatch Updates\nMembers\nList Administrators in a Chat\nGet the Number of Members in a Chat\nKick a Chat Member\nPromote a Chat Member\nRestrict a Chat Member\nOther\nMake an API Call\nAnswer an inline Query\nTroubleshooting\nHow to find out the ID of a private channel/group:\nHow to find out the user ID\nAdding Your Bot To the Channel:\nTesting a Public Channel\nTesting a Private Channel:\nRetrieving the ID From the Web Version of Telegram\nRegistration and Login\nMy bot is hitting limits, how do I avoid this?\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

send SMS, check messages status, check account balance and pricing, send a voice message, and lookup HLR, MNP, and CNAM information in your sms77 account.\n\nPrerequisites\n\nAn sms77 account\n\nIn order to use sms77 with Make, it is necessary to have an sms77 account. If you do not have one, you can create an sms77 account at sms77/signup.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting sms77 to Make\n\nTo connect your sms77 account to Make, you need to obtain your API Key.\n\n1. Login to your sms77 account.\n\n2. From the left menu, click Settings and then click HTTPS API.\n\n3. Copy the API Key to your clipboard.\n\n4. Go to Make and open the sms77 module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n5. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection and click Continue.\n\n6. In the API Key field, enter the API key copied in step 3.\n\n7. Click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nOther\nSend SMS\n\nSends one/multiple SMS to one/multiple user(s).\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your sms77 account.\n\n\n\n\nMessage\n\n\t\n\nEnter the message text.\n\n\n\n\nRecipient\n\n\t\n\nEnter the recipient's phone number.\n\n\n\n\nDebug\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether you want to send the SMS and charge the account:\n\nYes\n\nNo\n\n\n\n\nDelay\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date and time when you want to send the message. For example, 2016-03-04 23:25:04 or 1141511104.\n\n\n\n\nFlash\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to send SMS as a flash:\n\nTrue\n\nFlash\n\n\n\n\nFrom\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name or phone number that displays to the recipient.\n\n\n\n\nLabel\n\n\t\n\nEnter a label for the message to filter the messages when searching. For example, Marketing1.\n\n\n\n\nNo Reload\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to send duplicate SMS within a timeframe of 180 seconds:\n\nTrue\n\nFalse\n\n\n\n\nPerformance Tracking\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to active performance tracking for URLs found inside the message.\n\n\n\n\nTime to Live\n\n\t\n\nEnter the time in milliseconds after which you do not want the message to be delivered.\n\n\n\n\nType\n\n\t\n\nSelect the SMS type:\n\nEconomy\n\nDirect\n\n\n\n\nUser data Header (UDH)\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether to send SMS with custom User Data Header (UDH). monitor the event persons in your Swapcard account.\n\nTo use the Swapcard modules, you must have a Swapcard account. You can create an account at swapcard.com.\n\nRefer to the Swapcard API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Swapcard to Make\n\nTo establish the connection, you must:\n\nObtain your API key in Swapcard.\n\nEstablish the connection in Make.\n\nObtain your API key in Swapcard\n\nTo obtain your API key from your Swapcard account:\n\nLog in to your Swapcard account.\n\nNote: You must log in as an organizer by clicking Organizer button.\n\nIn the top right corner, click on your Profile icon > API Keys.\n\nClick Create a new key.\n\nEnter a key name and click Generate the key.\n\nCopy the API key value shown and store it in a safe place.\n\nYou will use this value in the API Key field in Make.\n\nEstablish the connection with Swapcard in Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Swapcard module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nIn the API Key field, enter the API key copied above.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Swapcard modules. Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationSlybroadcast\nSlybroadcast\n\nThe Slybroadcast modules allow you to send campaign audio files and audio URLs from your Slybroadcast account.\n\nWarning\n\nThis app is intended for use with standard Slybroadcast accounts (https://www.slybroadcast.com) only, not for international accounts (https://www.slybroadcast.com/international)\n\nGetting Started with Slybroadcast\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Slybroadcast account\n\nIn order to use Slybroadcast with Make, it is necessary to have a Slybroadcast account. If you do not have one, you can create a Slybroadcast account at slybroadcast.com.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Slybroadcast to Make\n\n1. Go to Make and open the Slybroadcast module's Create a connection dialog.\n\n2. In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\n3. In the Username and Password fields, enter your Slybroadcast account's username and password details, and click Continue.\n\nThe connection has been established.\n\nActions\nSend a Campaign with Audio File\n\nSends a Slybroadcast campaign with the audio file.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Slybroadcast account.\n\n\n\n\nName of Audio File\n\n\t\n\nSelect the audio file of the campaign you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nDate\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date on which you want to send the campaign. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nPhone Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the phone numbers separated by a comma to which you want to send the campaign audio file. This field is required if you are not providing any List ID.\n\n\n\n\nCaller ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Caller ID of the campaign. The caller ID appears within the recipient's voicemail box.\n\n\n\n\nMobile Only\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether this campaign file is only for the mobiles.\n\n\n\n\nDispo URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter your own URL if you wish to have your call status data posted back automatically.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the List ID to which you want to send the campaign audio file.\n\nSend a Campaign with Audio URL\n\nSends a Slybroadcast campaign with the audio URL.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Slybroadcast account.\n\n\n\n\nDate\n\n\t\n\nEnter the date on which you want to send the campaign audio URL address. See the list of supported date and time formats.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter the campaign audio URL address you want to send.\n\n\n\n\nPhone Number\n\n\t\n\nEnter the phone numbers separated by a comma to which you want to send the campaign audio file. This field is required if you are not providing any List ID.\n\n\n\n\nCaller ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter the Caller ID of the campaign. The caller ID appears within the recipient's voicemail box.\n\n\n\n\nMobile Only\n\n\t\n\nSelect whether this campaign file is only for the mobiles.\n\n\n\n\nAudio Format\n\n\t\n\nEnter the audio format. For example, .mp3, .WAV.\n\n\n\n\nList ID\n\n\t\n\nSelect the List ID to which you want to send the campaign audio file.\n\nMake an API Call\n\nPerforms an arbitrary authorized API call.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Slybroadcast account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter a path relative to https://www.slybroadcast.com/. For example: /gateway/vmb.json.php\n\nNote\n\nFor the list of available endpoints, refer to the Slybroadcast API Documentation.\n\n\n\n\nMethod\n\n\t\n\nSelect the HTTP method you want to use:\n\nGET to retrieve information for an entry.\n\nPOST to create a new entry.\n\nPUT to update/replace an existing entry.\n\nPATCH to make a partial entry update.\n\nDELETE to delete an entry.\n\n\n\n\nHeaders\n\n\t\n\nEnter the desired request headers. You don't have to add authorization headers; we already did that for you.\n\n\n\n\nQuery String\n\n\t\n\nEnter the request query string.\n\n\n\n\nBody\n\n\t\n\nEnter the body content for your API call.\n\nExample of Use - List Audio files\n\nThe following API call returns all the audio files from your Slybroadcast account:\n\nURL: /gateway/vmb.json.php\n\nMethod: GET\n\nBody:Key: c_method\n\nValue: get_audio_list\n\nMatches of the search can be found in the module's Output under Bundle > Body. In our example, 2 audio files were returned:\n\nSlybroadcast\nGetting Started with Slybroadcast\nConnecting Slybroadcast to Make\nActions\nSend a Campaign with Audio File\nSend a Campaign with Audio URL\nMake an API Call\nExample of Use - List Audio files\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationSMSAPI\nSMSAPI\n\nWith SMSAPI modules in Make, you can create, update, search, and delete contacts, manage contact group membership, watch new SMSs and callback reports, send text messages, and call APIs.\n\nTo get started with SMSAPI, create an account at smsapi.com.\n\nNote\n\nRefer to the SMSAPI documentation for the list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect SMSAPI to Make\n\nTo establish the connection:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add an SMSAPI module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nSelect SMSAPI OAuth in the Connection type dropdown.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click the Show advanced settings toggle and enter your Client ID and Client Secret credentials or choose Additional scopes to make custom API calls.\n\nTo obtain client credentials for SMSAPI, you must contact SMSAPI support. Refer to the OAuth2 webflow section of the SMSAPI documentation for more information. If required, use the following Redirect URI: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/smsapi.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, log in to your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more SMSAPI modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nSet Up SMSAPI Webhooks\n\nThis app uses webhooks to trigger a scenario when an event occurs instantly. All webhook modules have an instant tag next their name.\n\nTo set up a webhook, follow these steps:\n\nAdd the SMSAPI instant module to your scenario and click Create a webhook.\n\nOptional: Enter a name for the webhook in the Webhook name field.\n\nSelect the corresponding connection for the webhook in the Connection field.\n\nIf you added the Watch New Callback Report module, select the Callback Type.\n\nClick Save > Copy address to clipboard.\n\nLog in to your SMSAPI account.\n\nIn the left sidebar, click on API settings > Callback URLs.\n\nSelect the corresponding Type using the information below, paste the URL copied in step 5, and click Add.\n\nModule\n\n\t\n\nModule Callback Type\n\n\t\n\nType\n\n\n\n\nWatch New SMS\n\n\t\n\nN/A\n\n\t\n\nCallback address - Receive SMS\n\n\n\n\nWatch New Callback Report\n\n\t\n\nSMS DLR\n\n\t\n\nCallback address - SMS DLR\n\n\n\n\nBulk Messages\n\n\t\n\nCallback address - Bulk Messages\n\n\n\n\nShort Link Hits\n\n\t\n\nCallback address - Short Link Hits\n\nSMSAPI will now send data to Make through the webhook when the selected event occurs.\n\nBuild SMSAPI Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nSMS\n\nWatch New SMSs\n\nWatch New Callback Reports\n\nSend a Text Message\n\nContact\n\nSearch Contacts\n\nCreate a Contact\n\nManage Contact Group Memberships\n\nUpdate a Contact\n\nDelete a Contact\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nSMSAPI\nConnect SMSAPI to Make\nSet Up SMSAPI Webhooks\nBuild SMSAPI Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

You can use your Facebook, Google account or you can create an SMS Alert account at smsalert.co.in.\n\nNote\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting SMS Alert to Make\n\n1. Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationSkype\nSkype\n\nThe Skype modules enable you to monitor events, or send a message and download an attachment in your Skype account.\n\nGetting Started With Skype\n\nPrerequisites\n\nA Skype account (create an account at skype.com)\n\nMicrosoft Azure Account (create an account at azure.microsoft.com/free)\n\nNotice\n\nThe module dialog fields that are displayed in bold (in the Make scenario, not in this documentation article) are mandatory!\n\nConnecting Skype to Make\n\nTo connect your Skype account to Make, you need to create a bot and obtain the Microsoft App ID and password in your Microsoft Azure account.\n\nLog in to your Azure Portal.\n\nClick Create a resource.\n\nIn the top center search bar, type bot. From the drop-down list, select Azure Bot.\n\nClick the Create button.\n\nIn the Azure Bot form, provide the required information about your bot, as follows:\n\nBot handle\n\n\t\n\nEnter the name for your bot.\n\n\n\n\nSubscription\n\n\t\n\nSelect the Azure subscription you want to use.\n\n\n\n\nResource Group\n\n\t\n\nCreate a new resource group, or select an existing one.\n\n\n\n\nLocation\n\n\t\n\nChoose the geographic location for your resource group. It's usually best to choose a location close to you.\n\n\n\n\nPricing Tier\n\n\t\n\nSelect a pricing tier. You may update the pricing tier at any time. For more information, see Bot Service pricing.\n\n\n\n\nType of App\n\n\t\n\nSelect Multi Tenant from the drop-down.\n\n\n\n\nCreation type\n\n\t\n\nCreate a new Microsoft App ID.\n\nClick Review + create. When Microsoft successfully validates the new bot, click Create.\n\nGo to the new resource, and open Channels.\n\nChoose Skype and configure the app. Optionally, you can also configure the other settings in the dialog box, e.g., Disable adding of bot to group conversations option in the Groups tab. Close channel settings.\n\nClick Add to Skype in the Connected Channels list, and add the bot to your Skype contacts.\n\nOpen Configuration, where you will find the Microsoft App ID.\n\nClick Manage > + New client secret to create a password.\n\nCopy the password now.\n\nWarning\n\nThe password will not be visible again after you leave this page.\n\nGo to Make, and open the Skype module's Create a connection dialog. Click Add.\n\nEnter the Microsoft App ID (see step 9 above) and Password (see step 11 above) in the respective fields, and click the Continue button to establish the connection.\n\nThe connection has been established. You can proceed with setting up the module.\n\nTriggers\nWatch Events\n\nTriggers when a specified event occurs.\n\nThe webhook URL needs to be generated in Make and then added to resource settings in the Azure portal.\n\nAdd the Watch events module to your Make scenario. Select events you want to filter received data by.\n\nGenerate and copy the webhook URL.\n\nLog in to your Azure portal.\n\nOpen the desired resource settings, and paste the webhook URL you have copied in step 2 above in the Messaging endpoint field, and click Save.\n\nNow, every time the event occurs, the Watch event module in your Make scenario is triggered.\n\nActions\nDownload an Attachment\n\nDownloads an attachment file.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Azure account.\n\n\n\n\nURL\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the URL you want to download attachment file data from.\n\nSend a Message\n\nSends a message to the specified conversation.\n\nConnection\n\n\t\n\nEstablish a connection to your Azure account.\n\n\n\n\nConversation ID\n\n\t\n\nEnter (map) the ID of the conversation you want to send a message to. You can map the ID from the Watch events module.\n\n\n\n\nText\n\n\t\n\nEnter the text of the message that is sent from bot to user.\n\n\n\n\nText Format\n\n\t\n\nSelect the format of the message's text using one of these values: markdown, plain, or xml. For details about text format, see Create messages.\n\n\n\n\nAttachments\n\n\t\n\nAdd Attachment objects that define additional information to include in the message. For more details about attachments, refer to the Attachment Object documentation.\n\n\n\n\nActions\n\n\t\n\nAdd the action to apply. For more details about actions, refer to the Rich Cards documentation.\n\n\n\n\nService URL\n\n\t\n\nEnter the URL that specifies the channel's service endpoint. Set by the channel.\n\nSkype\nGetting Started With Skype\nConnecting Skype to Make\nTriggers\nWatch Events\nActions\nDownload an Attachment\nSend a Message\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

Building\nGlossary\nCommunity\nSupport\nAcademy\nBlog\nAPI documentation\nmake.com\nMake Help CenterAppsCommunicationSalesloft\nSalesloft\n\nWith Salesloft modules in Make, you can search for, create, retrieve, update, delete, and watch records and make API calls.\n\nTo get started with Salesloft, create an account at salesloft.com.\n\nNote\n\nRefer to the Salesloft API documentation for the list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Salesloft to Make\n\nTo connect the Salesloft app:\n\nLog in to Make, add a Salesloft module to a scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom application's Client ID and Client Secret values. To create these values, see the Create App ID and Secret for Salesloft section.\n\nClick Save.\n\nReview the authorization notice and click Authorize.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Salesloft modules. If your connection needs reauthorization, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nCreate App ID and Secret for Salesloft\n\nYou can create your own application and connect it to Make using the App ID and Secret values from the application.\n\nGo to your Salesloft OAuth applications page.\n\nClick Create New in the OAuth Applications section.\n\nEnter a name for the app, paste https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/salesloft in the Redirect URI field, choose the Application Type, and click Save.\n\nCopy the Application Id and Secret values and store them in a safe place. You will use your Application Id in the connection Client ID field and Secret in the connection Client Secret field.\n\nYou now have the client credentials to connect to Make.\n\nBuild Salesloft Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nRecords\nSearch Records\nCreate a Record\nGet a Record\nUpdate a Record\nDelete a Record\nOther\nMake an API Call\nWatch Records\nSalesloft\nConnect Salesloft to Make\nCreate App ID and Secret for Salesloft\nBuild Salesloft Scenarios\nRecords\nOther\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."

employees, groups, receptions, and calls in your Relatel account.\n\nTo use the Relatel modules, you must have a Relatel account. You can create an account at relatel.dk.\n\nRefer to the Relatel API documentation for a list of available endpoints.\n\nConnect Relatel to Make\n\nTo establish the connection in Make:\n\nLog in to your Make account, add a Relatel module to your scenario, and click Create a connection.\n\nOptional: In the Connection name field, enter a name for the connection.\n\nOptional: Click Show advanced settings and enter your custom app client credentials. For more information, refer to Relatel OAuth Guide.\n\nIf requested, use the following Redirect URI when creating your custom app: https://www.integromat.com/oauth/cb/relatel.\n\nClick Save to be redirected to the login page.\n\nIn the Email and Password fields, enter your Relatel account credentials.\n\nClick Save.\n\nIf prompted, authenticate your account and confirm access.\n\nYou have successfully established the connection. You can now edit your scenario and add more Relatel modules. If your connection requires reauthorization at any point, follow the connection renewal steps here.\n\nBuild Relatel Scenarios\n\nAfter connecting the app, you can perform the following actions:\n\nEmployees\n\nList Employees\n\nGet an Employee\n\nGet Currently Authenticated Employee\n\nUpdate an Employee\n\nUpdate Currently Authenticated Employee\n\nGroups\n\nList Groups\n\nGet a Group\n\nCreate a Group\n\nSend a Text Message to Group\n\nJoin a Group\n\nLeave a Group\n\nUpdate a Group\n\nReceptions\n\nList Receptions\n\nGet a Reception\n\nCalls\n\nWatch New Calls\n\nGet a Call\n\nOther\n\nMake an API Call\n\nRelatel\nConnect Relatel to Make\nBuild Relatel Scenarios\nPrev\nNext\n© 2024 Celonis Inc."
